# BetterDungeon Mobile Port - TODO & Testing Tracker

This document tracks the manual testing, adjustments, and fixes required to ensure all features of the BetterDungeon extension work beautifully on the mobile Android port.

## Feature Testing Checklist

Mark features as `[OK]` when fully tested and perfectly ported. If a feature is broken or requires mobile-specific adjustments, add notes below it explaining why.
Mark features as `[~OK]` when they are mostly working but need further adjustments
Mark features as `[~X]` when they are barely working and need major adjustments
Mark features as `[X]` when they are not working at all
Mark features as `[?]` when they can't be tested or are not applicable on mobile (e.g., keyboard shortcuts that don't exist on touch devices).

- [~OK] **Markdown Feature** (`markdown_feature.js`)
  - *Notes:* It seems that nothing much has changed since your last attempted fix. Let me walk you through what's going on:
    - Firstly, the Auto Apply on Adventure Start system does work, which is sweet. It correctly initalizes the Auto Apply system.
    - However, in regards to the Auto Apply system itself, it is peculiar in its behavior.
      - When you press the "Apply Instructions" button in the popup menu, it instantly says "Failed" but it still correctly initializes the Auto Apply system.
      - For the most part, the Auto Apply system itself works fine, but it does seem to think that the Author's Note doesn't exist. It will always attempt to create the Author's Note plot component even when it exists, and isn't able to paste anything into the component.
  - Just take a deep dive into the Auto Apply system, how it works, and how other files that use the system use it to make sure it's all consistent and functional.
- [~OK] **Command Mode** (`command_feature.js`)
  - *Notes:* Horizontal scroll now works — menu is capped to viewport width via `max-width: calc(100vw - var(--bd-menu-left) - 8px)`. Button padding reduced from 16px to 8px, font shrunk to 12px. All buttons are reachable via swipe. No scroll affordance indicator (gradient/shadow/arrow approaches all failed to render in WebView — removed for clean slate).
  - *Remaining:* Test that Command button works when tapped after swiping to it. If so, this feature can be marked OK.

- [~OK] **Notes Feature** (`notes_feature.js`)
  - *Notes:* So, our recent fix has correctly placed the Notes element in the right position on the Plot tab in the Settings, but funnily enough, it also attempts to place the element at the top of the Story Cards subtab and Details subtab in the Adventure tab. Our detection is too loose and could be smarter.
  - Additionally though, and this is a bigger issue, we can't actually modify the contents of the Notes element. We can tap it but it constantly kicks us out.
- [OK] **Better Scripts** (`better_scripts_feature.js`)
  - *Notes:* Shockingly works! No issues with Better Scripts. I'm just as surprised as you are. The UI is a bit small, but that's a smaller issue.
- [X] **Input History** (`input_history_feature.js`)
  - *Notes:* Conceptually interesting, but the feature still doesn't work. Your changes doesn't seem to have created any new UI element on the page that allows the Input History feature to be used. I like what you were trying to do but it doesn't seem to appear.

## Findings and Other Notes

Through my testing, I found a lot of interesting bugs and issues that have popped up. This give good insight to what may be going wrong with out features, and may even give insight to bugs that we may need to fix on the standard version of BetterDungeon.

### Input Box Displacement

This is an important update on this Input Box Displacement issue.
Turns out, it literally isn't our fault LOL
It's a bug with the mobile web version of AI Dungeon that has been reported but not fixed.
Thankfully, that means we don't have to do anything except wait it out.

## DOM Information

I have provided important DOM information that I've gathered while restricting the size of the viewport on web, so this should replicate our WebView behavior.
Do note I gathered this DOM information with BetterDungeon disabled. (With some exceptions to diagnose some odd BetterDungeon behavior with the mobile web formatting)

### Adventure Page

The adventure page is the main page of the game. It contains the story text, the input box, and the action buttons. The adventure page is where the user will spend most of their time.

### Settings Page

The Settings page typically opens to the side on standard web, but on mobile web, it takes up the width of the screen, covering the main page.

### Adventure Page with Text Input Box Open

This the Text Input Box I've referred to previously. This is the main way you interact with your story and is the element that a lot of scripts attempt to modify.
